The tracking capabilities are robust and allow us to view all major KPIs including revenue, new users, new customer acquisition, and more. The support team is always helpful and does a great job addressing any questions you have. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The platform itself isn't the most intuitive to use and doesn't have the best UI/UX. It takes some playing around to figure out how to grab certain data, see how affiliates are performing, etc. Overall, though, once you become familiar with the platform, it's easy to use. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5471096 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">We used to manage affiliates on a one-on-one basis which wasn't scalable or practical. Partnerize makes it easy to manage all our affiliates and track their performance on one platform. Their affiliate program network is also robust, which makes it easy to recruit and partner with new affiliates. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on The platform excels in offering a diverse range of reputable partners across various industries, coupled with powerful tracking and reporting tools. These features, combined with exceptional customer support, make Partnerize an invaluable asset for efficient and effective affiliate marketing. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">While Partnerize offers many strengths, it does have areas that could be improved. The platform might sometimes feel overwhelming for beginners due to its extensive features and options. Additionally, while there is a wide range of partners available, finding the perfect match can be time-consuming, and the commission structure might not always align with user expectations. Lastly, some users might find the reporting tools complex, requiring a learning curve to fully utilize their potential. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8973462 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize significantly simplifies the complexities of affiliate marketing. By providing a comprehensive platform, it eliminates the need for multiple tools, streamlining the process of finding, managing, and optimizing affiliate partnerships. This consolidation not only saves time but also enhances the effectiveness of marketing campaigns. Additionally, its robust analytics and reporting tools offer deep insights into campaign performance, aiding in data-driven decision-making. This leads to more efficient allocation of marketing budgets and higher ROI. As a result, Partnerize has become an indispensable tool in my affiliate marketing strategy, enabling me to grow my network and revenues more effectively. <span class="spht">Review collected by and </p><p class="formatted-text">- It is super confusing to navigate, as stated in other reviews. The reporting you see within the tool is not what you'll get invoiced. You must download transaction-level reports and roll them up by process date to determine your commission invoices. 
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">Support
</p><p class="formatted-text">- They're responsive when you opt for their elite service, but I've always felt like they miss the mark in terms of finding relevant affiliates, especially non-discount ones
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">Conversion Tracking
</p><p class="formatted-text">- My data engineering team and I have spent 6 months trying to figure out the best way to send reconciled files to Partnerize so that they can better estimate what conversions were attributed to affiliates. Suppose you don't police how your conversions are tracked. In that case, you might be overpaying due to: not canceling refunds, currency conversions, and paying out on codes that shouldn't be attributed to affiliates. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7804905 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">We use partnerize to manage our affiliate commissions and overall network. The main benefit of Partnerize products is that there's a central location to manage the entire program. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div This reviewer was offered a nominal incentive as thanks for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Review source: G2 invite on behalf of seller</div><div class="tag" title="This reviewer was offered a nominal incentive as thanks for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Incentivized Review</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-2"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2023-03-14" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2023-03-14">Mar 14, 2023</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/partnerize/reviews/partnerize-review-7830893"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Capable but lacks flexibility and support"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize is a solid tracking platform and can provide deep data. Integration can be straightforward and quick via a GTM template. An available API can be used to access data not surfaced via the product UI. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize does not score well on customer service. The support team was not helpful in diagnosing a complicated tracking issue and providing a solution. Our email implementation required support for multiple languages and grouping by language which was not well supported in the latest product update. There are some features not easily available via the available API. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7830893 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Tracking and commission payouts for referral traffic from affiliates, influencers, and other partnerships. Communications with these partners via email. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c I found some very good partners within multiple niches to work with at Partnerize. Support is good and answers questions quickly and clearly. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The interface. There is a lot of small text and clutter. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-6992752 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Finding business partners within sports and travel niches. The migration was seamless and Partnerize accommodated many of our bespoke needs. The client success team is very responsive and attentive. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Some of the reporting functionalities do not offer the needed customization for our business, but there are always ways around it.
